local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);
return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2);
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3);
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4);
	local F5 = elsModule(ELSModel.F5);
	local F6 = elsModule(ELSModel.F6);
	local F7 = elsModule(ELSModel.F7);
	local F8 = elsModule(ELSModel.F8);
	local LS1 = elsModule(ELSModel.LS1);
	local G1 = elsModule(ELSModel.G1);
	local G2 = elsModule(ELSModel.G2);
	local G3 = elsModule(ELSModel.G3);
	local G4 = elsModule(ELSModel.G4);
	local G5 = elsModule(ELSModel.G5);
	local G6 = elsModule(ELSModel.G6);
	local G7 = elsModule(ELSModel.G7);
	local G8 = elsModule(ELSModel.G8);
	local RS1 = elsModule(ELSModel.RS1);
	local K1 = elsModule(ELSModel.K1);
	local K2 = elsModule(ELSModel.K2);
	if enabled then
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					F1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F8(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.05)
					F1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F8(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.05)
					F1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F8(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.05)
					F1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F8(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.05)
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					G1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G8(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.05)
					G1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G8(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.05)
					G1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G8(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.05)
					G1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					G8(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.05)
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					LS1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));
					RS1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));
					wait(0)
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					K1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));
					K2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.06)
					K1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));
					K2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.06)
				end
			end)
		end)
	else
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
		F5(1)
		F6(1)
		F7(1)
		F8(1)
		LS1(1)
		G1(1)
		G2(1)
		G3(1) 
		G4(1) 
		G5(1) 
		G6(1) 
		G7(1) 
		G8(1) 
		RS1(1) 
		K1(1)
		K2(1)
	end
end

					K2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					wait(0.05)
					K1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));		
					K2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					wait(0.05)
					K1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));		
					K2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					wait(0.05)
					K1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));		
					K2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					wait(0.05)
					K1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));		
					K2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					wait(0.05)
					K1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));		
					K2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					wait(0.05)
					K1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));		
					K2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					wait(0.05)
					K1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));		
					K2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					wait(0.05)
					K1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));		
					K2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					wait(0.05)
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					LS1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));		
					RS1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));	
					wait(0.07)
					LS1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));		
					RS1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));	
					wait(0.07)
				end
			end)
		end)
	else
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
		F5(1)
		F6(1)
		F7(1)
		F8(1)
		LS1(1)
		G1(1)
		G2(1)
		G3(1) 
		G4(1) 
		G5(1) 
		G6(1) 
		G7(1) 
		G8(1) 
		RS1(1) 
		K1(1)
		K2(1)
	end
end



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local centre = brakelights.Centre;
	local top = brakelights.Top;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
		brakelights.Top.Material = smoothMaterial;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
		brakelights.Top.Material = smoothMaterial;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_14_Charger/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
local headlightState = script.Parent.Parent.State.Headlights;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Light.Enabled = true;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Light.Enabled = false;
			wait(0.5);
		end; 
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	else
		for _,v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = (headlightState.Value == true and neonMaterial or smoothMaterial);
		indicatorRear.Light.Enabled = headlightState.Value;
	end;
end;

    Reverselights (ModuleScript)

local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then

			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;

			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_Explorer/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS Explorer → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local elsModule = script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart;

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local frontb = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.FrontB);
	local frontt = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.FrontT);
	local mirror = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.Mirror);
	local sidef = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.SideF);
	local sideb = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.SideB);
	local rear = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.Rear);
	local reverse = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.Reverse);
	
	local mainside = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.MainSide);
	local mainfront = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.MainFront);
	local mainrear = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.MainRear);
	
	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				frontb(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				frontt(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				mirror(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				sidef(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				sideb(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				rear(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				reverse(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				mainside(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				mainfront(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
				mainrear(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					rear(0)
					mirror(0)
					reverse(1)
					mainrear(1)
					wait(0.45)
					rear(1)
					mirror(1)
					reverse(0)
					mainrear(0)
					wait(0.45)
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				frontb(1)
				frontt(1)
				sidef(1)
				sideb(1)
				mainside(1)
				mainfront(1)
			end)
		end)()

	else
		frontb(1)
		frontt(1)
		mirror(1)
		sidef(1)
		sideb(1)
		rear(1)
		reverse(1)
		mainside(1)
		mainfront(1)
		mainrear(1)
	end
end

					sidef(1)
					mirror(1)
					frontb(1)
					frontt(1)
					wait(0.04)
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					mainside(1, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					mainrear(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					wait(0.07)
					mainside(1)
					mainrear(1)
					wait(0.07)
					mainside(1, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					mainrear(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					wait(0.07)
					mainside(1)
					mainrear(1)
					wait(0.07)
					mainside(0, Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255))
					mainrear(1, Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255))
					wait(0.07)
					mainside(1)
					mainrear(1)
					wait(0.07)
					mainside(0, Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255))
					mainrear(1, Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255))
					wait(0.07)
					mainside(1)
					mainrear(1)
					wait(0.07)
					mainside(1, Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255))
					mainrear(0, Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255))
					wait(0.07)
					mainside(1)
					mainrear(1)
					wait(0.07)
					mainside(1, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					mainrear(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					wait(0.07)
					mainside(1)
					mainrear(1)
					wait(0.07)
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					mainfront(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					wait(0.07)
					mainfront(1)
					wait(0.07)
					mainfront(0, Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255))
					wait(0.07)
					mainfront(1)
					wait(0.07)
					mainfront(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255))
					wait(0.07)
					mainfront(1)
					wait(0.07)
					mainfront(0, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
					wait(0.07)
					mainfront(1)
					wait(0.07)
				end
			end)
		end)()
	else
		frontb(1,  Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
		frontt(1, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
		mirror(1, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
		sidef(1, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
		sideb(1, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
		rear(1, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
		reverse(1, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
		mainside(1, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
		mainfront(1, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
		mainrear(1, Color3.fromRGB(190, 104, 98))
	end
end


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_F-350/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_F-350/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_F-350/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_F-350/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				if v:FindFirstChild('Attachment') then
					v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = true;
				else
					v.Light.Enabled = true;
				end
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				if v:FindFirstChild('Attachment') then
					v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = false;
				else
					v.Light.Enabled = false;
				end
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			if v:FindFirstChild('Attachment') then
				v.Attachment.Light.Enabled = false;
			else
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end
		end;
	end;
end;

end;

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)

				F1(1)

				wait(0.02)

				F4(1)	
				wait(0.09)

				F1(1)

				wait(0.02)						
				
				F1(1)

				F4(1)	
				wait(0.09)

				F1(1)
				F2(1)
				F3(1)
				F4(1)	
				wait(0.02)					
			end
		end)		
		task.defer(function()
			while true do	
				D1(0);
				D2(1);				
				S1(0)
				S2(0)
				S3(1)
				S4(1)
				wait(0.09)
				
				D1(1);
				D2(1);				
				S1(1)
				S2(1)
				S3(1)
				S4(1)
				wait(0.02)				
				
				D1(0);
				D2(1);
				S1(0)
				S2(0)
				S3(1)
				S4(1)
				wait(0.09)

				D1(1);
				S1(1)
				S2(1)
				S3(1)
				S4(1)
				wait(0.02)						

				D1(0);
				D2(1);
				S1(0)
				S2(0)
				S3(1)
				S4(1)
				wait(0.09)

				D1(1);
				D2(1);
				S1(1)
				S2(1)
				S3(1)
				S4(1)
				wait(0.02)					

				D1(1);
				D2(0);
				S1(1)
				S2(1)
				S3(0)
				S4(0)
				wait(0.09)

				D1(1);
				D2(1);
				S1(1)
				S2(1)
				S3(1)
				S4(1)
				wait(0.02)						

				D1(1);
				D2(0);
				S1(1)
				S2(1)
				S3(0)
				S4(0)
				wait(0.09)

				D1(1);
				D2(1);
				S1(1)
				S2(1)
				S3(1)
				S4(1)
				wait(0.02)	

				D1(1);
				D2(0);
				S1(1)
				S2(1)
				S3(0)
				S4(0)
				wait(0.09)

				D1(1);
				D2(1);
				S1(1)
				S2(1)
				S3(1)
				S4(1)
				wait(0.02)					
			end
		end)		
		task.defer(function()
			while true do

				R2(0)
				R3(0)
				R4(0)
				wait(0.18)	
				
				R1(1)
				R2(1)
				R3(1)
				R4(1)
				wait(0.09)					
			end
		end)		

	else
		F1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		F2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		F4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		R1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		R2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		R3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

		S2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		S3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

		T2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

		T6(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
		T7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T8(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
		T9(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T10(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		D1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		D2(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
	end
end



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_Sprinter/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

	121

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights2;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = neonMaterial
		body.Headlights.Bottom.Material = neonMaterial
		body.Headlights.Bottom.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = smoothMaterial
		body.Headlights.Bottom.Material = smoothMaterial
		body.Headlights.Bottom.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:36
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

	--Front Lightbar lights

	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)

	local L2 = elsModule(ELSModel.L2)
	local L3 = elsModule(ELSModel.L3)
	local L4 = elsModule(ELSModel.L4)
	local L5 = elsModule(ELSModel.L5)
	local L6 = elsModule(ELSModel.L6)
	local L7 = elsModule(ELSModel.L7)
	
	--Rear Lightbar lights

	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2)
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)

	local R5 = elsModule(ELSModel.R5)
	local R6 = elsModule(ELSModel.R6)
	local R7 = elsModule(ELSModel.R7)

	local P2 = elsModule(ELSModel.P2)	
	
	if enabled then	
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do

			pcall(function()

				R2(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

				R8(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));																			
				wait(0.20)

				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);		
				wait(0.08)

				R3(0);
				R4(0);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);

				wait(0.20)

				R2(1);
				R3(1);
				R4(1);
				R5(1);
				R6(1);
				R7(1);
				R8(1);

		coroutine.wrap(function()

end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_Tahoe/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

	-18,
	0,
	26,
	46,
	61,
	76,
	101,
	121
};


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

    Reverselights (ModuleScript)

local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;

	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do

			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;

		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Ambulance_Service/BCAS_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Ambulance Service → BCAS Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_Arrowboard_F-150/Body/Bed/weldBedServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    weldBedServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Arrowboard F-150 → Body → Bed
    Parent: Bed
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local platform = script.Parent.Parent.Parent.Chassis.Platform;
local platformCFrame = platform.CFrame;

local pivot = script.Parent.Pivot_1;
local pivotCFrame = pivot.CFrame;

local main = script.Parent.Pivot;
local mainCFrame = main.CFrame;

local board = script.Parent.Main;
local boardCFrame = board.CFrame;

local newInstance = Instance.new;

local descendants = script.Parent:GetDescendants();
for i = 1, #descendants do
	local v = descendants[i];
	if v:IsA('BasePart') and v ~= main and v.Name ~= 'Pivot_1' and v.Name ~= 'Main' then
		local w = newInstance('Weld');
		w.Part0 = board;
		w.Part1 = v;
		w.C1 = v.CFrame:Inverse() * boardCFrame;
		w.Parent = board;
		v.Anchored = false;
	end;
end;

local boardWeld = newInstance('Weld');
boardWeld.Name = 'BoardWeld';
boardWeld.Part0 = board;
boardWeld.Part1 = pivot;
boardWeld.C1 = pivotCFrame:Inverse() * boardCFrame;
boardWeld.Parent = board;
script.Parent.Main.Anchored = false;

local w = newInstance('Weld');
w.Name = 'BoardWeld';
w.Part0 = platform;
w.Part1 = main;
w.C1 = mainCFrame:Inverse() * platformCFrame;
w.Parent = platform;
main.Anchored = false;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_Arrowboard_F-150/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Arrowboard F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_Arrowboard_F-150/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Arrowboard F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_Arrowboard_F-150/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Arrowboard F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_Arrowboard_F-150/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Arrowboard F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_Arrowboard_F-150/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Arrowboard F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

	local I3 = tdModule(ELSModel.I3);

	local E2 = tdModule(ELSModel.E2);
	local E3 = tdModule(ELSModel.E3);
	local LD1 = tdModule(ELSModel.LD1);
	local LD2 = tdModule(ELSModel.LD2);

	local LU2 = tdModule(ELSModel.LU2);

	if enabled then
		ELSModel.C1:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.I1:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.I2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.I3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.E1:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.E2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.E3:SetAttribute('TD', true);

		ELSModel.LD2:SetAttribute('TD', true);

		while true do
			I1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));

			E3(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));

			LD2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			LU1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			LU2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));

			I2(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I3(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			C1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			E1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			E2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			E3(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			LD1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			LD2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			LU1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			LU2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			wait(0.2);
			I1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I2(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			I3(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			C1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			E1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			E2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			E3(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));

			LU1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
			LU2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));

			LU2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_Covered_F-150/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Covered F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_Covered_F-150/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Covered F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

	-18,
	0,
	26,
	46,
	61,
	76,
	109,
};


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_Covered_F-150/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Covered F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Covered F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_Covered_F-150/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Covered F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_Covered_F-150/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Covered F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_Covered_F-150/Config/Modules/TdPart.lua ---

--[[
    TdPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Covered F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_F-350/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_F-350/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_F-350/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_F-350/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_F-350/Config/Modules/TdPart.lua ---

--[[
    TdPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_F-350_Wrecker/Body/Boom/BoomWeldServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    BoomWeldServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA F-350 Wrecker → Body → Boom
    Parent: Boom
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local Vertical = script.Parent.Vertical;

local Main = script.Parent.Main; --Acts like platform part

local HookPivot = script.Parent.HookPivot --This connects the hook section to the vertical moving pivot
local HookMain = script.Parent.Hook.HookMain; --Connects hookpivot to the hook section

local function WeldParts(part0: BasePart, part1: BasePart, name: string?): Weld
	local weld = Instance.new('Weld');
	weld.Parent = part0;
	weld.Part0 = part0;
	weld.Part1 = part1;
	weld.Parent = part0;
	weld.Name = name or 'Weld' 
	weld.C1 = part1.CFrame:Inverse() * part0.CFrame;
	return weld;
end

WeldParts(Main, Vertical, 'VerticalWeld');

for _,v in next, script.Parent.WeldToVertical:GetChildren() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') then
		WeldParts(Vertical, v);
	end;
end;

for _,v in next, script.Parent.Nuts:GetChildren() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') then
		WeldParts(Vertical, v);
	end;
end;

WeldParts(Vertical, HookPivot, 'VerticalHookPivotConnection');

WeldParts(HookPivot, HookMain, 'HookPivot/MainConnection');

local hook = script.Parent.Hook;
local extension = hook.Hook.Extension;

WeldParts(HookMain, extension, 'ExtensionWeld');

for _,v in next, script.Parent.Hook.Hook:GetChildren() do
	if v:IsA('BasePart') then
		WeldParts(extension, v, v.Name..'ToExtension');
	end
end;

local clampFront = hook.Hook.ClampFront;

local function WeldClamp(clamp)
	local pivot = clamp.Pivot;
	local cylinder = clamp.Cylinder;
	local clampPart = clamp.Clamp;
	local rotatingPart = clamp.Rotate;
	
	WeldParts(pivot, rotatingPart);
	WeldParts(rotatingPart, clampPart);
	WeldParts(clampFront, cylinder);
	WeldParts(clampFront, pivot, `{clamp.Name}PivotToExtension`);
end;

WeldClamp(hook.LeftClamp);
WeldClamp(hook.RightClamp);

	--Front Lightbar lights
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1)
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2)
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3)
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4)
	local T5 = elsModule(ELSModel.T5)
	local T6 = elsModule(ELSModel.T6)
	local T7 = elsModule(ELSModel.T7)
	local T8 = elsModule(ELSModel.T8)
	local T9 = elsModule(ELSModel.T9)
	local T10 = elsModule(ELSModel.T10)

	--Front Lightbar lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2)
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)
	local R5 = elsModule(ELSModel.R5)
	local R6 = elsModule(ELSModel.R6)
	local R7 = elsModule(ELSModel.R7)
	local R8 = elsModule(ELSModel.R8)
	local R9 = elsModule(ELSModel.R9)

		T1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
		T2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
		T3(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));

		T6(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
		T7(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
		T8(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));

		T10(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));

		R2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));
		R3(1, Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61));

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_F-350_Wrecker/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA F-350 Wrecker → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_F-350_Wrecker/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA F-350 Wrecker → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_F-350_Wrecker/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA F-350 Wrecker → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_F-350_Wrecker/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA F-350 Wrecker → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_F-350_Wrecker/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA F-350 Wrecker → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_Flatbed_TowTruck/Body/Bed/weldBedServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    weldBedServer (Script)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Flatbed TowTruck → Body → Bed
    Parent: Bed
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local platform = script.Parent.Parent.Parent.Chassis.Platform;
local platformCFrame = platform.CFrame;

local main = script.Parent.Main;
local mainCFrame = main.CFrame;

local newInstance = Instance.new;

local descendants = script.Parent:GetDescendants();
for i = 1, #descendants do
	local v = descendants[i];
	if v:IsA('BasePart') and v ~= main then
		local w = newInstance('Weld');
		w.Part0 = main;
		w.Part1 = v;
		w.C1 = v.CFrame:Inverse() * mainCFrame;
		w.Parent = main;
		v.Anchored = false;
	end;
end;

local w = newInstance('Weld');

w.C1 = mainCFrame:Inverse() * platformCFrame;
w.Parent = platform;
main.Anchored = false;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_Flatbed_TowTruck/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Flatbed TowTruck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_Flatbed_TowTruck/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Flatbed TowTruck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_Flatbed_TowTruck/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Flatbed TowTruck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;
	local sidelights = body.Bed.Orange
	local frontLights = headlights.Front;

	if enabled then

		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
		end;
		
		for i, v in next, sidelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
		end;		

		for _,v in next, frontLights:GetChildren() do
			if v:IsA('Beam') or v:IsA('SpotLight') then
				v.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;

		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
		end;
		for i, v in next, sidelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
		end;
		for _,v in next, headlights.Front:GetChildren() do
			if v:IsA('Beam') or v:IsA('SpotLight') then
				v.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_Flatbed_TowTruck/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Flatbed TowTruck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/British_Columbia_Automobile_Association/BCAA_Flatbed_TowTruck/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → British Columbia Automobile Association → BCAA Flatbed TowTruck → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:37
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;
